 Dariya safina tayi "ai sai ki daure ki haifo mana, hmm guda dayan ma ya aka ciki cwt balle uku, yau ban ga kin zo schl ba shine nace ko jikin ne".


 "Kafafuna ne suka rike tun safe shiyasa".

"Ina Amira take?" 
 "Gatacan a kitchen"
 "To agaisheta sannan a gaida baby da babansa".

 "To zasuji, sai nazo ganin takwarata".

 
Yanzu ta kai ga kullum Faisal na gidan safiyya sabida ya shawo kan Amira, amma yarinyar nan taki, in ma yazo ya ya ganta a waje to haka zata shige ciki ta barshi nan, wani lokaci har sai safiyya inta leko ne take ganinsa. Tayi fama da ita har ta gaji dan da ta fara mata maganarshi sai ta hau kuka wai ita ba aure zatayi yanzu ba karatu zata fara.


 Sati daya kenan shima kanshi duk yayi wani iri kaman ba Faisal dan gayu ba, Ranar dai da daddare ya taso alhaji suka taho gidan, lokacin sufyan na nan, Suna falo dukkansu yana matsawa safiyya kafanta daya rike ita kuma tana cin popcorn.


 Sallama akayi sufyan ya mike ya fita, gaisawa sukayi da alhaji cikin sakin fuska kaman ba shi ba, sufyan ya bude musu dayan falon suka shiga.


 "Da farko dai ina mai Baku hakuri akan abinda yafaru, kuma dai ni na daukeshi matsayin kaddara, nayi matukar farin ciki da Faisal yazomin da wannan zance sai yacemin wai kuma yana fuskantar problem daga gun ita yarinyar"

 "Nace masa dole ya fuskanci matsala tunda dai ga abinda ya faru, to shine Nazo da kaina dan Allah a taimaka mana, wallahi yaron nan ko abin cin kirki baya ci haka hajiya ke fama dashi wurin aiki dama ya dena zuwa kullum yana daki kamar maraya".


 Sufyan ya danyi murmushi "eh to alhaji nima dama mai dakina tagayamin abinda ke faruwa, to sai na ce mata sai abinda yarinya tace da mahaifiyarta, amma dai nima insha'allahu zan yi iya bakin kokarina sannan zanje nasamu mahaifiyarta ".


 Alhaji yama sufyan godiya sannan suka tafi. Koda ya koma lokacin Amira tana daki sai yake gayawa safiyya suwaye sukazo.

 "Yanzu alhaji da Kansa yazo nan".

 Sufyan ya kalleta yana dariya "sai ma kingashi sima yazama nagari".


 Dariya sukayi dukkansu yace ta kira masa Amira.

 "Yanzu alhaji da Faisal suka bar gidan nan akan maganarki, inaso inji daga bakin ki dan naji auntyn ki tace tanata fama dake kinki".

Amira kanta a Kasa" yaya ni fa karatu zan fara kaga, ni yanzu gaskiya ba aure zanyi ba, kuma ni ni bana....".


 Safiyya ta dariya tana girgiza kai, sufyan yace " ai Amira aure bai hana karatu baga auntyn ki nayi ba yanzu, na tabbata bazakiyi Dana sani akan Faisal ba sabida nasa anmin bincike akan shekaran jiya kuma an tabbatar min yanzu yadaina halayensa na banza dayakeyi kuma kullum sallahr jam'i yanzu bata wuceshi, ki yi tunani mana Amira".


Hawaye tafarayi "yaya kaima yanzu kabiyewa Anty ta daina sona kun koma kan Faisal, yarinya dani za'amin aure".


 Mai safiyya zatayi banda dariya,sufyan ya kalli Amira yana murmushi "kyale antynki kinji Amira, ni ina bayan ki amma kuma wannan shi ne son dazamu nuna miki , in yarinya tasamu mai sonta na gari to ayimata aurenta sai ta cigaba da karatun acan. Kuma na tabbata Faisal zai barki ki cigaba.


 Yanzu dai tashi ki tafi kiyi shawara,zan nemeki.safiyya dai sai dariya take sufyan na binta da kallo " da yanzu zance miki ina bukatar ki sai kice min cikinki na ciwo amma ji dariyar dakikeyi sofy".



 Wanshekare sufyan ya nufi gombe wurin inna da zancen Amira.


 Koda tagama sauraren zancen sufyan shiru 
Yaga tayi tana binsa da ido.

 "Inna baki ce komai ba, ni dai nasan tabbas yaron da mahaifinsa sunyi hankali kuma nayi bincike a Kansu sosai, insha allahu alherine za'a kulla".

  Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke tana mai murmushi " sufyanu ni me zance bayan 'ya a wurin Ku take, nidai lubabatu nabaku daman zabawa Amira mijin daya dace da ita ko bayan raina Amira takuce kaida mai dakinka, komai nata na gunku, Allah ya saka muku da alheri".

 A nan kuma Kaduna ranar saiga hajiya kulu (mahaifiyar Faisal) ita zo gidan sofy. Sun tarbeta hannu biyu biyu itada Amira suka cika gabanta da kayan tarban baki.

 Safiyya ta numfasa "to hajiya wallahi muma muna bakin kokarin mu wajen ganin ta saurareshi ,kuma insha allahu zata sauko ,domin yarinyace mai hakuri ,da ikon Allah komai zai wuce Don shima mijin nawa yau ya tafi wajen mahaifiyar ta ne da zancen".

Amira tayi mata godiya sannan hajiya ta fita.


 Bayan fitan tane safiyya ke cewa Amira dan Allah tayi hakuri ta yarda da auren nan insha allahu bazatayi Dana sani ba",

_wannan nakune mutanen *the three* wato 'ya'yan Anty Sis, tundaga kan, lubiee, lubna,benazir, jeedah ,miemie bee, queen miemie, Yar ficika dai dai sauransu, Allah ya barmu tare cikin aminci,ILYSM_


 
Safiyya a ranar ta kira Faisal tayi masa albishir, aiko duk ya rikice mata a waya. Wanshekare ko gama breakfast basuyiba daya ke Saturday ne lokacin ma sufyan bai fita ba sai gashi yazo gidan.


 Safiyya sai dariya take masa,sufyan ne yafita ya sameshi a waje sukayi maganan Cewar gobe ya turo da magabatan sa a ayi magana kawai. Faisal yayi masa godiya sannan safiyya ta tura masa Amira.


 Ansan lokaci biki nan da wata uku, dan haka sai shirye shirye duk gidajen biyu sukeyi. Yayinda inna tazo ta dauki Amira ta suka tafi can kafancan wato garinsu sukayi sati biyu sannan suka Sanar da kowa maganar biki.


 Gyara kuwa iri iri safiyya kewa Amira, Momy ma ta aiko musu dashi, jikin nan sumul inka ganta tayi kyau. An kawo kayen lefan ranar su safina duk sunzo domin ita yanzu sofy zama da kyar ne tashi da kyar. Kowa ya kalleta sai yace "sannu kinji, Allah ya raba lafiya". Shima kanshi sufyan din tausayi take basa shiyasa ya hanata yin komai a gidan yace a turo mata da kuyanga daya daga gidan sarki.


 Biki saura kwana biyu akayi sisters eve Wanda safiyya ta shirya, amarya ansha kyau sai hotuna ke tashi, itadai safiyya tana daga zaune sai dai kallo domin lokacin cikinta watanni takwas kenan da kwanaki.


 A na gobe biki akayi kamu a alhaji sani dauda multipurpose hall dake nan unguwan rimi, ango ya iso da jama'arsa ansha rawa sannan an zubar da kudi.


  Wanshekare ranar juma'a  misalin karfe daya da rabi aka daura auren a masallaci, gidan safiyya a cike ta ko'ina, Momy tazo itada umma ranar. Su Anty Amina dama an Dade da zuwa itada cwt.


  Duk Inda safiyya zatabi kyaji Momy na fadin "yi ahankali kinji auta, sannu fa sannu".

 Safiyya sabida tsabar gajiya duk tayi jaa kafafunta su kunbura. Daukan waya tayi ta kira sufyan , shagwaba ta fara masa wai yazo batajin dadi, da Sauri ya shigo ta bayan dakinsa.


 Lokacin tana falo Suna magana da inna, tasowa tayi ta nufi dakinsa, da Sauri taje ta rungumesa yana shafa bayanta "sofy meke damunki ne".


  Janta yayi suka zauna akan gado tana kwance jikinsa, shagwabe fuska tayi "kawai wallahi bacci nakeji kafafuna duk sun rike".


 Kallonta yayi yadda tayi kyau cikin wani material Fari da baki, sai kamshi takeyi, zame dankwalin kanta yayi ya shaki kamshin dake fita a kanta "banace kar ki wahalar da kanki ba tunda bakida lafiya k
 sofy".

 Kara shigewa jikinsa tayi "to dear zan bar baki ne nazauna a daki ,ai Kasan dai dole na fito".

 Wayarsa ce tayi ringing ya dauka, yayin da bacci yayi awon gaba da ita a jikinsa duk ta cukwikwiyeshi da malunmalun dinsa.


 Da yake wasu souvenirs din adakinsa suke dan haka safina tashigo dakin, dariya ta hau yi " Momy na can na cigiyarta Ashe tana nan makale da miji".


 Ya sufyan yamata nuni da hannu datayi a hankali kar ta tashi, dariya tayi ta dauki abinda zata dauka ta fita. Haka ya zauna tanata bacci yana mammatsa mata jiki har karfe hudu sannan ta farka.


 Murmushi ta masa yace "tashi kiyi wanka ko kyaji dadin jikin ki".

 Shi ya taimaka mata tayi wanka ta sauya wasu kayan sannan ya kira safina a waya cewan ta kawo mata abinci. Saida ta cika ciki sannan ya wuce masallaci ita kuma ta koma gun baki.


 Da daddare akazo aka wuce da amarya gidan hajiya kulu domin a can zata kwana gobe sai a wuce da ita gidan mijinta dake unguwan sunusi.


 Wanshekare da Momy zasu wuce ta kira sufyan "dama kan maganar dawo da yarinyar nan gida haihuwa ne, Kasan wata na Tara kenan cikin nan nata kuma dai nafari ne, dan haka ko zamu tafi da ita ne yau".

 Sufyan ya tsugunnar da kai Kasa "Momy da kin barta anan bayan ta sauka sai ta koma, Allah duk wata kulawa ina bata agida".

 Momy ta bude baki "to sannu gwanin iya kula, ko bakaga Amina da safina da suka cikin ya tsufa Suma dawowa dasu gida mukayi ba, wannan Abu wajibi a gunmu kuma dole ta dawo gida in cikinta ya tsufa, domin duk kulawar dazaka bata bata kai tamu ba, zan iya maka uziri yau sabida tanada baki ,amma yanzu kawai kagaya min ranar dazaka kawomin ita".


 Kanshi a Kasa yace "nan da sati mai zuwa insha allahu zan kawota".


 "Yawwa ko kaifa sufyanu, kana ganin yarinya kaman ciki zai fasata Don girma, Allah dai ya sauketa lafiya".

 "Amin amin"


 Satin na zagayowa sufyan ya dauketa sai gombe, Momy sai nan nan take da ita dan kuwa bata komai a gidan nan, har ruwan wanka sai dai Momy ta Tara mata a roba ta kaimata komai take bukata. Kawai matsalanta daya kafafunta da suke kumbura kuma dama sufyan ke matsa mata su yanzu kuma bata iya Cewa Momy ta matsa mata.


 Kullum Suna makale a waya yana gaya mata yadda yayi missing dinta,dama duk weekend a gidan Momy yakeyi.


 Kayan jarirai iri iri ba Wanda basu Siya ba, in yazo shi ke kaita asibiti, lokacin da aka mata scanning tace kar a gaya mata mace ne ko namiji nurses din sai dariya suke mata wai maman twins ce ita.


  Ranar da yamma sungama suna waya da sufyan yake cemata "sofy bakyajin dadi muryarki duk ta canza".

 Murmushi tayi dan kuwa jun kugun ta take kaman ba'a jikinta yakeba "lafiya ta kalau dear banajin komai".

  Haka ta daure sunata hira har ta kashe wayar , kiran Amira ne ya shigo ta dauka "aunty har yanzu shiru".

 "Uhm amira amarya, kona haihu ai nasan bazai barki kizo gombe ba sabida amarci.

 Amira ta shagwabe mata fuska kaman tana gabanta "haba aunty ai wallahi ko akafa sai Nazo , shima kullum sai yayi zancen haihu warki".

 nan dai tadinga cijewa har sukagama wayar da Amira, Momy ce ta leko ta ganta kwance alamun tana bacci, kashe mata wuta tayi sannan tayiwa jakadiya magana Cewar sofy fa na ciki dan kuwa ita ke kwana da ita.


 Tanajin Momy kawai shiru tayi dan yadda kwankwason ta ke juyawa abunka da haihuwar Fari batason ya ciwon nakudan yakeba.

  Da Sauri jakadiya ta shigo dakin tana fadin "subhanallahi, sannu bari na taso Momy".,


 Fita tayi da Sauri ta isa side din daddy tana knocking, da Sauri Momy ta fito jin cewan safiyya ba lafiya.

 Da daddy ne ya fito da mota momy da jakadiya 
Suka kama safiyya wacce bakin ta ya mutu dan ciwo.


 Asibitin su safwan aka wuce da ita, Momy tasa waya ta kirashi Cewar ya zo asibiti gashi nan sun kawo safiyya batajin dadi.


 Suna zuwa aka wuce da ita labour room ,ganin yadda taketa wahala yasanya Momy hawaye, cikin Sauri safwan ya iso bai tsaya sun gaisa dasu momy ba ya shige dakin da aka kaita.


 Daddy ya matso ya zaunar da Momy kusa dashi sabida yadda takasa tsaye takasa zaune, kallon agogo suka kalla lokacin karfe goma da rabi na dare. Shiru suka zauna har karfe sha daya da rabi, jikin Momy da jakadiya duk ya gama sanyi ganin ba Wanda ya fito daga dakin da aka shigar da sofy.


 Safwan ne ya fito da sauri Momy ta isa garesa "safwan ina autar takene?".

 Murmushi yamata ganin yadda ta damu "Momy 'yan biyu ne, munyi munyi takasa haihuwa, dan haka zamu shigar da ita dakin theater ne".


 Momy ta fara kuka, daddy ya kalli safwan "OK Allah ya sauke ta lafiya, Allah yasa ayi a sa'a. Kayi signing kawai".


 Cikin kuka momy ta kallesu "a kira mijinta a gaya masa".

 Daddy ya jata suka zauna "bai kamata a kirasa cikin Daren nan ba, kiyita mata addu'a kinga keta gado, da twins zata fara".

 Hawayen idonta ta goge ta danyi murmushi "Allah ya rabasu lafiya".


 Gangaro da ita akayi suka wuce da ita, minti biyu da shigarsu sai ga wata nurse ta fito da Sauri ta nufo Momy "ina kayan dakukazo dashi?".

 Momy ta miko mata basket din kayan ,pad da pant kawai ta dauka ta koma ciki da Sauri. 

 Sai gashi an kara  gangaro da ita, safwan na rike da baby daya itama nurse na rike da baby daya.

Momy ta karaso da Sauri tana binsu har aka shigar da ita resting room. Momy ta riko hannunta tana murmushi "auta! Auta!! Sannu kinji".


 Safwan ne ya shigo shida dady kowanne da guda daya a hannunsa. Safwan ya mikawa Momy na hannunsa ta amsa tana hamdala "wai har anyi aikinne".

 "A ah muna shiga kuma cikin ikon Allah saiga haihuwan gadan gadan".

 Daddy ya yiwa safiyya sannu "gashi an haihu baban yara baiji ba".

 Momy tayi dariya "wai  na hannunka mace ce ko namiji ,ni nan dai namiji ne".

 Safwan yayi dariya "ai duk mazane , Momy saikin zaba Wanda yamiki".

 Dariya sukayi dukkansu yayinda safiyya baccin wuya yayi gaba da ita.


 Safwan shi ya kira sufyan ya mishi albishir. Yayi yayi yagaya masa mace ne ko namiji safwan ya kiya, yace "inkazo zakaga ko mace ce ko namiji".


 Flight ya biyo zuwa gombe, lokacin 'yan Uwa sai zuwa suke dan ance sai ta kwana  za'a sallameta.


 Ta tashi kenan Momy ta hada mata tea tana sha, anty Amina na rike ba daya sai ga sufyan ya shigo, yana sanye da suit Baka da wando, yayi kyau da ka Ganshi zaka gane angon karni ne.



  Kusa da ita ya zauna yana mai gaida momy, kallonta yayi hade da kashe mata ido daya , shagwabe masa fuska tayi.


 Daukan babyn dake gefenta yayi ya zuba masa ido, Anty Amina ta mika masa dayan "ga dayan nan ya sufyan".

 Bude ido yayi sosai bakin sa a bude dan farin ciki "au guda biyu ne, masha Allah, sannu sofy".


 Aunty Amina tayi dariya itada momy, duk ya daukesu ya makalkale yama rasa maizaice, safina ce ta shigo tana fadin "maman twins".

   Dariya sukayi ta karaso ta dauki daya tana fadin "wai gaskiya an gaisheki cwt, wannan luba K
Luban yara".

 Nan Momy ke sheda musu ai da aiki za'a mata cikin ikon Allah kuma ta haihu da kanta.

 Sufyan bai samu ya gana da sofy ba sabida mutane, wanshekare kuwa aka sallamota gida. Ranar Amira ta iso sai murna take kaman zata shigar da yaran ciki.


  Sai da daddare ne jama'a suka lafa sufyan ya taddata a daki tana feeding daya.
 Zuwa yayi ya zauna ya dauki dayan "wannan dani yake kama".

 Murmushi tayi ,"wanene babba ne a cikinsu , ya tambayeta bayan ta miko masa dayan , momy tace wannan ne babba ta nuna Wanda yafi hasken.

 Jingina jikinta tayi a jikinsa ya yimata kiss a goshi "Allah ya miki albarka sofy, Allah ya barmu tare har karshen rayuwar mu, Allah yasa ke matatace har a aljanna".

 Murmushi tayi "amin my dear".

 Kallonta yayi "dama ranar dazaki haihu inajin yadda kike magana na gane, sannu lallai kin sha aiki sofy na".

 
 Murmushi ta mishi tana kallon baban Wanda ya ke kama sosai da sufyan domin har hasken sa yadauko karamin kuma shi bai kai babban haske ba.

 Hura mata iska yayi a fuska bayan ya gama yi musu addu'a, ta lumshe idonta "wani Suna kikeso asamusu maman twins?".

 "Ni duk Wanda Kasa musu yayi dadyn twins".

 Murmushi yayi "to bari na musu khudba da sunan mai martaba da daddy, yayi".

 "Yayi Allah ya musu albarka".

 Daga mata gira yayi "kinga shekara mai zuwa sai ki haifo mai sunan umma da Momy".

 Waro ido tayi "aniyarka ta bika, ai ban manta ba".

 Dariya yadinga mata ita kuma ta mike Don ji Momy na kiranta tazo anyi baki 'yan barka.



 Ranar Suna yaran sukaci Abubakar da uthman (hussain da hassan). Sunan da yayi armashi Don ba karamin kashe kudi akayi ba, mai martaba yabawa yaran dawakai, safiyya ansha kyau.

 Faisal ma yazo shida hajiya, Amira taje ta shigo dasu, itama kana kallonta Kasan tana amarci sabida yadda ta cika.

 Dama jiya safina tagama mata tsiyan wai ciki gareta. Anty Sis da mutanenta ansha ashobi, yaran dai sunyi goshi masha Allah.


  Haka sofy ta zauna cikin kula wajen Momy itada twins, yayinda sufyan zai wuce aikin hajji shida aunty Amina da safwan. Amira ita kuma da Faisal zata tafi. 

 Bayan haihuwanta da kwanaki goma suka wuce. Kullum tana makale dashi a waya yayinda Momy ke tsumata da kayan gyra iri iri. Yaran bul bul sunashan hotuna gun mutane, itama kusan kullum sai ta ai ka masa da pics dinsu.


 Ranar hasan arfa haka ta zauna gaban TV tanata kallo ,gani takeyi kaman zata ganshi. Haka sukayi babbar sallah cikin farin ciki yayinda sofy keta shirin komawa gida domin yanzu yaran watansu biyu kenan gwanin ban sha'awa.


 Ana jibi zai dawo ta koma  tare da kuyangarta daya mai suna maimuna bayan an gyare mata gidanta tsaf, ranar da zai dawo duk gidan ya dauki kamshin girki Dana turare.

 Ta shirya tsaf itada twins, cikin red and black dukkansu. Ita sanye take da Riga da zani wash ready made masu kyau. Rigar mai laushi baka sai zani red anyi masa kwalliya da stones baki. Sai ta kashe dauri da dankwalin red shima , tasha Jan lalle da baki sai kamshinta take mai tadawa da sufyan hankali.


 Khalil shi ya kawoshi gida, yana shigo wa ta rungumeshi batasan ma tare da ya Khalil sukeba. Bakinsa ta kama tafara mishi salonta na barka da zuwa. Dayake yafita tsayi sai ya kama kugunta ya dagata da kyau.

 Khalil na ganin haka ya aje masa kayansu ya juya yana dariya. A kasa suka zube ganin abun nayi ne, daukanta yayi zuwa dakinsa suka gaisa da kyau, soyayya suka sha kaman zasu cinye juna tama manta da su hussain a falo.


 Yana rungume da ita sai murmushi yake mata, murya can Kasan makoshi yace "sofy... I miss u, ina yarana".

 
 Karamin yatsanta tasa tana zagaye dashi a kirjinsa  "miss u too swthrt, yaranka Suna nan suma sunyi missing naka, kataso muje kayi wanka tukun sai akawo maka su".



 Tare sukayi wanka sannan ta shiryasa, koda taje falo ta tarar maimuna ta kwashe su. Shiga wurinta tayi tana jiyo kukan hassan "ayyah my baby , maimuna shine baki kawo min su ba",

 Dariya maimuna tayi "ai Anty inata kwankwasa kofan baki ji ba".

 Murmushu safiyya tayi sannan ta kwashesu ta nufi dasu gun sufyan, yama rasa wanne zai dauka, kamar ya lashe su. Duk sunyi wayau sai bangala mishi dariya sukeyi.

 Tare sukaci abinci sai anan ya tuna cewan fa tare da Khalil yake "sofy na mance fa tare da Khalil muka zo".

 Safiyya ta zuba masa dambun naman plate tana dariya "aiko ya tafi,ni ban ma saniba".

 Kashe mata ido yayi "ai ke dince kin rikitani dayawa".

 Kada kwayan  idonta tayi tare da lashe lebanta "nuna maka nayi kenan ba karamin missing dinka nayi ba".


  Nan ya dinga amsa wayoyi anata mishi sannu dazuwa, cikin satin baya fita ko'ina sai soyayya dasuke sha, danma masu sannu da zuwa na musu cikas.



 Safiyya ta shirya taje gidan Amira, ba karamin murna tayi ba, tarasa Inda zata sasu itada twins, itama ga 'dan cikin ta nan ya kunno kai. Sun sha hira dan a gidan ta wuni sai dare sufyan yazo ya kwashe su.



 Twins Nada shekara daya sufyan ya shirya musu zuwa kauyen su papa, abinda yamusu dadi shine samun su papa sun musulunta dan kuwa bayan tafiyan sufyan wani yazo kauyen kuma musulmine dan haka gunsa suka anshi musulunci.


 Sunyi matukar farin cikin ganinsu , sai daukan twins sukeyi musamman Camila, sufyan ya basu kudi sosai da sosai sannan ya ce zasu dinga ganawa ta waya domin sun kulla zumunci kenan.


 Daga nan suka wuce Kasa mai tsarki sukayi ummara sannan suka dawo Nigeria. Gombe suka sauka gidan umma , daganan suka shiga gidan Momy.


 Anty Amina tazo tanata fama da tsohon ciki , itama safina ranar sunzo nan suka zauna sunata hira, twins daga wannan ya rugo ya fada kan safiyya sai wannan ya zo ya cukwikwiyeta.


 Momy ta dinga dariya ,"lalle kina fama auta da sojoji a gidanki".



 Kwanansu biyu suka koma Kaduna, wanshekare itama Amira tazo da yarta safiyya suka musu sannu da zuwa. Ranar da daddare safiyya bayan ta kwantar da twins ta iso wurin sufyan daketa danne danne a system.

 Bayanshi taje ta rungume ta manna masa kiss , lumshe ido yayi "sofy bazaki barni na karasa aikin nan ba ko zaki tsokanoni".

 Mirginoshi tayi ya fado jikinta tana murmushi "to ni bacci nakeji fa".


 Kwaikwayan muryanta yayi "to bari nazo kinsan ni bana jiran a kirani, Allah yasa yau nayi sa'a nasamun ma su twin sister".

 Dukanshi tayi a kirji "badai a cikin nan nawaba, wollah ban mance ba".


 Kashe mata ido yayi "OK. Ba matsala sai na karo yan mata 'yan shekaru 16 suzo suyita zazzagemin yara tunda ke kin kiya".


 Tureshi tayi ta hade fuska, janyo ta yayi ya fara haukata ta da soyayyarshi, sai da komai ya lafa ya ke rada mata a kunne "kece ta farko a zuciyata safiyya, kuma insha allahu kece ta karshe, zuciyata taki ce na mallaka miki ita hade da gangar jikina duka, kece jinin  jikina ke ce hasken idona kuma uwar 'ya'yana, ina sonki safiyya ta".


 Kankameshi tayi itama ta rada masa a kunne " Kaine rayuwana ya sufyan, luv yhu too swthrt".
